-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Table structure for table `tbl_absence_cdl`
--

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `tbl_absence_cdl` (
  `code_absence` int(10) NOT NULL auto_increment,
  `code_inscription` varchar(25) collate utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL default '',
  `code_cours` varchar(25) collate utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL default '',
  `comptabilise` varchar(5) collate utf8_unicode_ci default NULL,
  `n_comptabilise` tinyint(4) NOT NULL default '0',
  `n_incomptabilise` tinyint(4) NOT NULL default '0',
  `date` date NOT NULL default '0000-00-00',
  `jeton` varchar(3) collate utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL default '',
  `horaire` varchar(25) collate utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL default '',
  `nombre` smallint(6) NOT NULL default '0',
  `annee_academique` varchar(25) collate utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL default '',
  `session` varchar(25) collate utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL default '',
  `archive` binary(1) NOT NULL default '0',
  PRIMARY KEY  (`code_absence`),
  KEY `code_inscription` (`code_inscription`),
  KEY `code_inscription_2` (`code_inscription`,`annee_academique`,`session`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM  DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci AUTO_INCREMENT=3784 ;
